 After the introduction of Goods and Services Tax (GST) in the country, there will be a slight reduction in the price of fertilizer
 kendriya mantri anant kumaar ne shuukravaar ko yah baat kahi
 He said that after the GST rate on fertilizer has been reduced from 12 percent to five percent, the price of fertilizer will fall
 sarkaar kaa yah nirnay kisaanon ke hit main liya gaya
 Union Chemicals and Fertilizers Minister Anant Kumar told reporters here that the new reduced rate of GST will reduce the burden of Rs 1,261 crore on farmers
 tippaniyan He said that the reduction in GST rate from the earlier 12 percent to 5 percent would reduce the prices of urea, DAP, MOP and other mixed fertilizers marginally
 unhone daawa kiya ki urvarak par jiesti kii kam kii gai dar se gramin kshetra main samruddhi aegi
 (from input language) unhone kaha ki urvarak par jiesti dar ko 12 pratishat se ghataakar paanch pratishat kar die jane ke baad urvarak ke daam main yah giravat aegi
 This decision of the government was taken in the interest of farmers
 kendriya rasayan evam urvarak mantri anant kumaar ne yahaan patrakaron se kaha ki jiesti kii nai ghati dar se kisaanon par 1,261 karod rupee kaa boj kam hoga
 The comments unhone kaha, jiesti dar ko pehle ke 12 pratishat se ghataakar 5 pratishat kiye jane se uria, diapi, emopi or duusare mishrit urvarkon ke daam maamuli rup se kam honge
 He claimed that the reduced rate of GST on fertilizer will bring prosperity to the rural sector
 (input bhashaa se) Union Chemicals and Fertilizers Minister Anant Kumar told reporters here that the new reduced rate of GST will reduce the burden of Rs 1,261 crore on farmers
 tippaniyan He said that the reduction in GST rate from the earlier 12 percent to 5 percent would reduce the prices of urea, DAP, MOP and other mixed fertilizers marginally
 unhone daawa kiya ki urvarak par jiesti kii kam kii gai dar se gramin kshetra main samruddhi aegi
